name:Sâ€iâ€lâ€eâ€nâ€câ€eâ€sâ€kâ€yâ€s
info:Deluxe Hot Spring Room Suite - Mountain-View
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:62 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:Many people have a misunderstanding about this hotel, thinking that since it is such an expensive luxury hotel in the Huangguoshu Waterfall Scenic Area, naturally there are many rooms that can directly see the waterfall. In fact, it is not the case. Among the three hotels in the scenic area, only some rooms of Qianshouju can see the waterfall, but it is also quite far away. The only room that can see the waterfall in Bailian is the waterfall-viewing suite, which is actually not in the hotel and needs to be taken by car. The price is also quite expensive at 50,000 per night.
.
So, if you stay in this hotel, you donâ€™t have to be obsessed with the waterfall view. If you want more cost-effectiveness, the next floor of the waterfall-viewing suite is a tea room. You can spend a thousand yuan to have afternoon tea and sit there for an afternoon. Of course, no matter how good the scenery here is, it is just a distant view, which is far less shocking than walking through the Water Curtain Cave in the scenic area.
.
This time, I stayed in the Lake View Hot Spring Suite of Bo Lian, which is nominally 120 square meters and is on the second floor of the villa. From the overall experience, it is not as good as the rooms of the same level in Chongqing and Tengchong Bo Lian. Although Huangguoshu is the newest Bo Lian and the style used can indeed reflect the style of Bo Lian, the design language is obviously not elegant enough and a little dull. It is also because the ceiling is a little low and not transparent enough.
.
The living room is right after the door. The terrace is directly opposite the reception area. There is also a connecting door on the right hand side to form a double bedroom suite. The welcome gift is a little simple, some seasonal loquats. There are mini bars on both sides of the door. There are 2 raw and 2 cooked tea bags in the iron can. The quality is not bad. There is a capsule coffee machine with 6 capsules. There are 8 bottles of water in the cabinet below. The small refrigerator is free but there is not much content, and no customized service can be provided, because they are all sugary drinks, which is equivalent to nothing for me. The hotel actually said that there is no sugar-free cola and soda water to replace it. For this price, it is really not right, and many hotels now provide sugar-free drinks.
.
The living room is generally square, monotonous, and unremarkable, with no extra decoration. The large connected terrace outside is equipped with lounge chairs and parasols, a dining table, and then the hot spring pool. It is called a lake view, but it is actually a small pond dug by the hotel itself. There are black swans and red carp swimming in it, and the plants are lush. The landscape is average. You can reach the other side from the road in the park, but you can't see the hot spring pool. The privacy is still good.
.
The hot spring pool was already circulating water when I checked in. There were some candlesticks and essential oils at night. There were enough bath salts and rose petals. The body feeling was also good. You can control the water temperature by yourself.
.
The bedroom is not large. There is a desk by the window and a sofa coffee table facing the hot spring pool. The lack of a stool at the end of the bed does reduce the body feeling. There is a night bed service but it is not complete. The hot spring pool is arranged, but the consumables used are not replenished.
.
Going into the bedroom, there is a cloakroom with a dressing table on the left, and a master bathroom on the right, with double basins but no bathtub. The space is still a bit cramped. The Kohler smart toilet and Hansgrohe shower are old and not suitable for a hotel that opened in 2019. The supplies used are good, the Leilabo 33, but there is no soap, and the hair dryer is Dyson.
.
In general, this lake view suite is a bit monotonous and boring, and there is a big gap between it and the Tengchong Bailian with transparent lighting and the Chongqing Bailian with its own river view swimming pool. If you only want a private bath, the Qianshouju next door will be more cost-effective.
----------------------------------------

msg:There is no need to say much about the brand of Bailian. Products produced by Bailian must be high-quality! I personally think that except for the high price, there should be no other disadvantages. ğŸ˜‚

The room we booked is a room with a private hot spring. I stayed with my parents. We booked a twin room, but the hotel did not ask us to add any fees. I think it is very nice in this regard. ğŸ˜‚

The hot spring left me with a particularly good impression of this hotel. Another is their superior geographical location. They can provide a service such as exclusive and Huangguoshu afternoon tea. You can sit alone in a high-rise building in an exclusive space to quietly and beautifully appreciate the Huangguoshu Waterfall, while enjoying afternoon tea and watching the beautiful scenery. Another good thing is that they will provide two tickets to the Huangguoshu Waterfall scenic area, and provide car pick-up and drop-off services. This is actually very friendly for families who bring the elderly to play. It is also very happy for children to come and play, because there are many hot spring pools in the public area, and children can play batik and take away one of their own works for free. In addition, there is a welcome gift, which is very ceremonial. Tea is served and a silver necklace of the Miao ethnic group is given to the guests. My parents are very happy and have been wearing it all the time. Although it is just a decoration, it is fun!

Tickets to Huangguoshu Scenic Area/Sightseeing Bus: Included in the room rate, and a car pick-up and drop-off service is also provided.
Unlimited outdoor garden hot springs for two people: There are many hot spring pools, which are very fun.
Round-trip pick-up service between Anshun West High-speed Railway Station/Huangguoshu Airport: We drove there by ourselves, so there is no need for pick-up and drop-off, but this service is really very good. I saw a family of six coming, and the hotel arranged a business car to pick them up. Very convenient.

Overall, it was a very good vacation, and my parents were very satisfied!
